<script is:inline>
  // Show sticky CTA after scrolling past hero, with dismiss support
  (function() {
    const sticky = document.getElementById('sticky-cta');
    const dismissBtn = document.getElementById('sticky-cta-dismiss');
    if (!sticky) return;
    let dismissed = false;
    let ticking = false;
    window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
      if (dismissed) return;
      if (!ticking) {
        requestAnimationFrame(function() {
          sticky.classList.toggle('is-visible', window.scrollY > window.innerHeight * 0.8);
          ticking = false;
        });
        ticking = true;
      }
    });
    dismissBtn?.addEventListener('click', function() {
      dismissed = true;
      sticky.classList.remove('is-visible');
    });
  })();
</script>

<!-- Contact form handling -->
<script is:inline>
(function(){
  var form = document.getElementById('contact-form');
  if (!form) return;
  var btn = document.getElementById('form-submit-btn');
  var successEl = document.getElementById('form-success');
  var errorsEl = document.getElementById('form-errors');

  form.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    errorsEl.hidden = true;
    var errors = [];
    var parentName = form.querySelector('[name="parentName"]');
    var studentName = form.querySelector('[name="studentName"]');
    var email = form.querySelector('[name="email"]');
    var phone = form.querySelector('[name="phone"]');
    var level = form.querySelector('[name="studentLevel"]');
    if (!parentName.value.trim()) errors.push('Parent name is required');
    if (!studentName.value.trim()) errors.push('Student name is required');
    if (!email.value.trim() || !/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email.value)) errors.push('Valid email is required');
    if (!phone.value.trim()) errors.push('Phone number is required');
    if (!level.value) errors.push('Student level is required');
    if (errors.length) {
      errorsEl.innerHTML = errors.join('<br>');
      errorsEl.hidden = false;
      return;
    }
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.innerHTML = '<span>Sending...</span>';
    fetch(form.action, {
      method: 'POST',
      body: new FormData(form),
      headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json' }
    }).then(function(r) {
      if (r.ok) {
        successEl.hidden = false;
        form.reset();
        btn.disabled = false;
        btn.innerHTML = '<span>Sent!</span>';
      } else {
        errorsEl.textContent = 'Something went wrong. Please try again or WhatsApp us.';
        errorsEl.hidden = false;
        btn.disabled = false;
        btn.innerHTML = '<span>Find Out How We Can Help</span>';
      }
    }).catch(function() {
      errorsEl.textContent = 'Network error. Please try again or WhatsApp us.';
      errorsEl.hidden = false;
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.innerHTML = '<span>Find Out How We Can Help</span>';
    });
  });
})();
</script>

<!-- Parallax scroll effect on orbs -->
<script is:inline>
(function(){
  if (window.matchMedia('(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)').matches) return;
  var bars = document.querySelectorAll('.result-bar-fill');

  // Animate result bars when visible
  var barObserver = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
    entries.forEach(function(entry) {
      if (entry.isIntersecting) {
        entry.target.style.width = entry.target.style.getPropertyValue('--bar-width');
        barObserver.unobserve(entry.target);
      }
    });
  }, { threshold: 0.3 });
  bars.forEach(function(bar) { barObserver.observe(bar); });
})();
</script>

<!-- Immersive 3D particle canvas -->
<script is:inline>
(function(){
  if (window.matchMedia('(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)').matches) return;
  var c = document.getElementById('hero-canvas');
  if (!c) return;
  var ctx = c.getContext('2d');
  var dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
  var W, H;
  var mouseX = 0.5, mouseY = 0.5;
  var particles = [];
  var PARTICLE_COUNT = 120;

  function resize() {
    W = c.parentElement.clientWidth;
    H = c.parentElement.clientHeight;
    c.width = W * dpr;
    c.height = H * dpr;
    ctx.setTransform(dpr, 0, 0, dpr, 0, 0);
  }
  resize();
  window.addEventListener('resize', resize);

  // Create particles at different depth layers
  for (var i = 0; i < PARTICLE_COUNT; i++) {
    var depth = Math.random(); // 0 = far, 1 = near
    particles.push({
      x: Math.random() * 2 - 0.5,
      y: Math.random() * 2 - 0.5,
      z: depth,
      baseX: Math.random() * 2 - 0.5,
      baseY: Math.random() * 2 - 0.5,
      size: 1 + depth * 2.5,
      speed: 0.0002 + depth * 0.0005,
      drift: Math.random() * Math.PI * 2,
      alpha: 0.08 + depth * 0.25,
      hue: Math.random() > 0.65 ? 30 : 210, // gold or blue
    });
  }

  // Mouse / touch tracking
  document.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e) {
    mouseX = e.clientX / window.innerWidth;
    mouseY = e.clientY / window.innerHeight;
  });
  document.addEventListener('touchmove', function(e) {
    if (e.touches[0]) {
      mouseX = e.touches[0].clientX / window.innerWidth;
      mouseY = e.touches[0].clientY / window.innerHeight;
    }
  }, { passive: true });

  var startTime = performance.now();

  function draw(now) {
    var elapsed = now - startTime;
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);

    // Background atmosphere — subtle radial glow that follows mouse
    var gx = W * (0.3 + mouseX * 0.4);
    var gy = H * (0.3 + mouseY * 0.4);
    var grad = ctx.createRadialGradient(gx, gy, 0, gx, gy, W * 0.7);
    grad.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(43,90,140,0.08)');
    grad.addColorStop(0.5, 'rgba(212,133,58,0.03)');
    grad.addColorStop(1, 'transparent');
    ctx.fillStyle = grad;
    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, W, H);

    // Draw particles with parallax depth
    var mx = (mouseX - 0.5) * 2;
    var my = (mouseY - 0.5) * 2;

    for (var i = 0; i < particles.length; i++) {
      var p = particles[i];
      // Organic drift
      p.drift += p.speed;
      var driftX = Math.sin(p.drift) * 0.02 * (1 + p.z);
      var driftY = Math.cos(p.drift * 0.7) * 0.015 * (1 + p.z);

      // Parallax: deeper particles move less
      var parallaxX = mx * p.z * 0.08;
      var parallaxY = my * p.z * 0.08;

      var px = (p.baseX + driftX + parallaxX + 0.5) * W;
      var py = (p.baseY + driftY + parallaxY + 0.5) * H;

      // Wrap around
      if (px < -20) px += W + 40;
      if (px > W + 20) px -= W + 40;
      if (py < -20) py += H + 40;
      if (py > H + 20) py -= H + 40;

      // Depth-based glow
      var s = p.size;
      var a = p.alpha;

      // Pulse subtly
      a *= 0.7 + 0.3 * Math.sin(elapsed * 0.001 + p.drift);

      if (p.hue === 30) {
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(212,158,80,' + a + ')';
      } else {
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(100,150,200,' + a + ')';
      }

      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.arc(px, py, s, 0, Math.PI * 2);
      ctx.fill();

      // Glow for near particles
      if (p.z > 0.6) {
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(px, py, s * 3, 0, Math.PI * 2);
        if (p.hue === 30) {
          ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(212,133,58,' + (a * 0.15) + ')';
        } else {
          ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(43,90,140,' + (a * 0.12) + ')';
        }
        ctx.fill();
      }
    }

    // Draw faint connection lines between nearby particles
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(43,90,140,0.04)';
    ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
    for (var i = 0; i < particles.length; i++) {
      var p1 = particles[i];
      var p1x = (p1.baseX + Math.sin(p1.drift) * 0.02 + (mx * p1.z * 0.08) + 0.5) * W;
      var p1y = (p1.baseY + Math.cos(p1.drift * 0.7) * 0.015 + (my * p1.z * 0.08) + 0.5) * H;
      for (var j = i + 1; j < particles.length; j++) {
        var p2 = particles[j];
        var p2x = (p2.baseX + Math.sin(p2.drift) * 0.02 + (mx * p2.z * 0.08) + 0.5) * W;
        var p2y = (p2.baseY + Math.cos(p2.drift * 0.7) * 0.015 + (my * p2.z * 0.08) + 0.5) * H;
        var dx = p1x - p2x;
        var dy = p1y - p2y;
        var dist = dx * dx + dy * dy;
        if (dist < 15000) {
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(p1x, p1y);
          ctx.lineTo(p2x, p2y);
          ctx.stroke();
        }
      }
    }

    requestAnimationFrame(draw);
  }
  requestAnimationFrame(draw);
})();
</script>

<!-- Programme Quiz Logic (#8) -->
<script is:inline>
(function(){
  var quiz = document.getElementById('programme-quiz');
  if (!quiz) return;
  var answers = {};

  quiz.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    var btn = e.target.closest('.quiz-option');
    if (!btn) return;
    var step = btn.closest('.quiz-step');
    var stepNum = step.getAttribute('data-step');
    answers[stepNum] = btn.getAttribute('data-value');

    // Highlight selected
    step.querySelectorAll('.quiz-option').forEach(function(b){ b.classList.remove('selected'); });
    btn.classList.add('selected');

    var next = btn.getAttribute('data-next');
    if (next === 'result') {
      setTimeout(function(){ showResult(); }, 300);
    } else {
      setTimeout(function(){
        step.hidden = true;
        var nextStep = quiz.querySelector('[data-step="' + next + '"]');
        if (nextStep) nextStep.hidden = false;
      }, 300);
    }
  });

  function showResult() {
    quiz.querySelectorAll('.quiz-step').forEach(function(s){ s.hidden = true; });
    var result = document.getElementById('quiz-result');
    var title = document.getElementById('quiz-result-title');
    var desc = document.getElementById('quiz-result-desc');
    var isIndividual = answers['3'] === 'individual';
    var isJunior = answers['1'] === 'sec1-2';
    var isJC = answers['1'] === 'jc';
    var isEcons = answers['1b'] === 'econs';
    var link = document.getElementById('quiz-result-link');

    if (isIndividual) {
      title.textContent = 'One-to-One Coaching';
      desc.textContent = 'Tailored individual sessions focused on your child\'s specific needs. Flexible scheduling with personalised feedback — SGD 120–140/session.';
      link.href = '/programmes/';
    } else if (isJC && isEcons) {
      title.textContent = 'H2 Economics';
      desc.textContent = 'Rigorous A-Level Economics preparation covering micro and macro. Diagram precision, essay technique, and case study mastery — from SGD 360/month.';
      link.href = '/h2-economics/';
    } else if (isJC) {
      title.textContent = 'H1 General Paper';
      desc.textContent = 'A-Level GP preparation using the SHARP Method\'s legal-analytical framework. Argumentation, critical reading, and essay writing across all content themes — from SGD 360/month.';
      link.href = '/h1-general-paper/';
    } else if (isJunior) {
      title.textContent = 'Sec 1-2 English Foundation';
      desc.textContent = 'Build a strong analytical foundation early. 90-minute weekly sessions in small groups of 6 — SGD 280/month.';
      link.href = '/o-level-english/#sec1-2';
    } else {
      title.textContent = 'Sec 3-4 O-Level Intensive';
      desc.textContent = 'Exam-focused preparation with monthly mock grading. Master every O-Level component with the SHARP Method — SGD 320/month.';
      link.href = '/o-level-english/#sec3-4';
    }
    result.hidden = false;
  }

  var restart = document.getElementById('quiz-restart');
  if (restart) {
    restart.addEventListener('click', function(){
      answers = {};
      document.getElementById('quiz-result').hidden = true;
      quiz.querySelectorAll('.quiz-step').forEach(function(s){ s.hidden = true; });
      quiz.querySelector('[data-step="1"]').hidden = false;
      quiz.querySelectorAll('.quiz-option').forEach(function(b){ b.classList.remove('selected'); });
    });
  }
})();
</script>

<!-- Social Proof Ticker (#10) -->
<script is:inline>
(function(){
  var ticker = document.getElementById('proof-ticker');
  if (!ticker) return;
  var messages = [
    { text: 'A parent in Singapore just enrolled their child for O-Level English tuition', time: '2 hours ago' },
    { text: 'New 5-star Google review received', time: '5 hours ago' },
    { text: 'A Sec 4 student just scored A2 on their mock paper', time: 'Yesterday' },
    { text: 'A family in Tampines signed up for the free assessment', time: '1 day ago' },
    { text: 'New enrolment from Jurong East — Sec 2 student', time: '2 days ago' },
    { text: 'A parent left a 5-star review: "Transformative teaching"', time: '3 days ago' },
    { text: 'Currently 47 students enrolled across all programmes', time: 'Live' },
    { text: 'Next intake opens June 2026 — 8 slots remaining', time: 'Updated today' },
  ];
  var idx = 0;

  function showNext() {
    idx = (idx + 1) % messages.length;
    var item = ticker.querySelector('.proof-ticker-item');
    item.style.opacity = '0';
    item.style.transform = 'translateY(8px)';
    setTimeout(function(){
      item.querySelector('.proof-ticker-text').textContent = messages[idx].text;
      item.querySelector('.proof-ticker-time').textContent = messages[idx].time;
      item.style.opacity = '1';
      item.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
    }, 400);
  }

  setInterval(showNext, 5000);
})();
</script>

<!-- Audience Toggle -->
<script is:inline>
document.querySelectorAll('.audience-btn').forEach(function(btn) {
  btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
    document.querySelectorAll('.audience-btn').forEach(function(b) { b.classList.remove('active'); });
    btn.classList.add('active');
    var audience = btn.dataset.audience;
    document.getElementById('msg-parent').hidden = audience !== 'parent';
    document.getElementById('msg-student').hidden = audience !== 'student';
  });
});
</script>

<!-- Diagnostic Quiz -->
<script is:inline>
(function() {
  var answers = {};
  var step = 1;
  var totalSteps = 4;

  document.querySelectorAll('.diag-quiz-opt').forEach(function(btn) {
    btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
      answers['q' + step] = btn.dataset.value;
      btn.closest('.diag-quiz-step').querySelectorAll('.diag-quiz-opt').forEach(function(b) { b.classList.remove('selected'); });
      btn.classList.add('selected');

      setTimeout(function() {
        var current = document.querySelector('.diag-quiz-step[data-step="' + step + '"]');
        current.classList.remove('active');
        step++;

        var progressBar = document.getElementById('diag-quiz-progress-bar');
        if (progressBar) progressBar.style.width = ((step - 1) / totalSteps * 100) + '%';

        if (step <= totalSteps) {
          var next = document.querySelector('.diag-quiz-step[data-step="' + step + '"]');
          if (next) next.classList.add('active');
        } else {
          showDiagQuizResult();
        }
      }, 300);
    });
  });

  function showDiagQuizResult() {
    var result = document.getElementById('diag-quiz-result');
    var title = document.getElementById('diag-quiz-result-title');
    var text = document.getElementById('diag-quiz-result-text');
    if (!result || !title || !text) return;

    var grade = answers.q2;

    if (grade === 'A') {
      title.textContent = 'Your child is close to excellence';
      text.textContent = 'With targeted refinement on exam technique, the jump to A1 is very achievable. The SHARP Method (especially step P — Practise via retrieval) focuses on the precise skills examiners reward at the top bands.';
    } else if (grade === 'B') {
      title.textContent = 'Strong potential — a structured approach will unlock it';
      text.textContent = 'B4-C5 students often know the content but lose marks on technique. SHARP gives them a five-step process to convert knowledge into exam marks — See, Hit, Apply, Refine, Practise.';
    } else if (grade === 'C') {
      title.textContent = 'Significant improvement is possible';
      text.textContent = 'With the right foundation work and exam strategies, C6-D7 students typically see a 2-grade improvement within one term at A-Worthy.';
    } else {
      title.textContent = 'We can help turn this around';
      text.textContent = 'Our small class size (max 6) means your child gets the individual attention they need. We start with a diagnostic to identify exact gaps, then build up systematically.';
    }

    result.hidden = false;
    if (document.getElementById('diag-quiz-progress-bar')) {
      document.getElementById('diag-quiz-progress-bar').style.width = '100%';
    }
  }
})();
</script>

  <section class="prog-section" id="lesson-structure">
    <div class="container">
      <p class="eyebrow">Every Lesson</p>
      <h2 class="prog-section__heading" data-animate="reveal-up">Inside a SHARP lesson &mdash; the 60 minutes that change how your child thinks</h2>

      <div class="card-grid card-grid--2">
        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="1">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">See (5 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Your child learns to read questions the way a lawyer reads a brief &mdash; identifying exactly what is being asked, what type of response is required, and where the marks lie. No more losing marks to misread questions.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="2">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">Hit (15 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">The tutor models expert-level analysis on a live example, then your child selects the right framework &mdash; Core Move or ACED for English, P-E-E-L for GP, DEED for Economics &mdash; and targets the highest-value marks first.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="3">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">Apply (15 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Your child writes a full response using the claim-evidence-reasoning framework &mdash; with the tutor providing immediate, targeted feedback. No waiting until next week to find out what went wrong.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="4">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">Refine (10 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Your child self-assesses against the SHARP checklist, then receives process-level feedback &mdash; not just what was wrong, but exactly why and how to fix it. Every answer is polished to exam standard.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="5">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">Practise (15 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Your child tackles a fresh question independently, applying everything from the lesson. Every session ends with one concrete improvement goal for the week.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </section>

    <div class="container">
      <p class="eyebrow">1128 Syllabus</p>
      <h2 class="prog-section__heading" data-animate="reveal-up">Complete GCE O-Level English Language (1128) Syllabus Coverage</h2>
      <p class="prog-section__sub">Every component of the GCE O-Level English Language syllabus (1128), taught with precision and exam alignment.</p>

      <div class="card-grid card-grid--2">

          <h3 class="prog-card__title">Paper 1 &mdash; Writing</h3>

            <li>Visual text comprehension</li>
            <li>Narrative and non-fiction comprehension</li>
            <li>Literal, inferential, and evaluative questions</li>
            <li>Summary writing (80-word paraphrase)</li>
            <li>Editing (grammar and vocabulary correction)</li>
            <li>Oral Communication (video stimulus response)</li>
          </ul>
        </div>

  <!-- ===== OUR APPROACH ===== -->
  <section class="prog-section" id="approach">
    <div class="container">
      <p class="eyebrow">The SHARP Method</p>
      <h2 class="prog-section__heading" data-animate="reveal-up">Why the SHARP Method produces O-Level English results other approaches can&rsquo;t</h2>

      <div class="card-grid card-grid--2">
        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="1">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">See (5 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Most students lose marks because they misread what the question is really asking. Your child learns to decode every question type &mdash; comprehension, situational writing, essay prompt &mdash; before putting pen to paper. No more careless misinterpretations.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="2">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">Hit (10 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Once the question type is clear, your child selects the right framework: Core Move for inference, ACED for comprehension responses, CAPS for composition planning, STAMP CARD for situational writing. The right tool for the right question &mdash; every time.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="3">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">Apply (20 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Whether it&rsquo;s a narrative essay, a formal letter, or a comprehension response, your child applies the chosen framework to write a structured answer. Live writing practice with immediate tutor feedback &mdash; not corrections returned a week later when the moment has passed.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="4">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">Refine &amp; Practise (15 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">The steps that turn B-grade students into A-grade students. Your child self-checks every response against a systematic checklist, then practises via retrieval until the process is automatic &mdash; catching the grammar slips, missing content points, and weak conclusions that silently drag marks down.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="5">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">STAMP CARD &mdash; Editing</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Subject-verb, Tense, Articles, Modifiers, Prepositions, Conjunctions, Apostrophes, Run-ons, Determiners. The mnemonic gives your child a systematic sweep through every error category in the editing section, so the 10 marks examiners hand out for accuracy are no longer left on the table.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="6">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">ACED &mdash; Paper 2 Visual Text</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Audience, Content, Effect, Design. ACED breaks down every visual-text question into the four dimensions examiners credit &mdash; who the text targets, what it claims, how the design persuades, and what it achieves. No more guessing at flyer or poster questions.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- ===== INSIDE A LESSON ===== -->
  <section class="prog-section lesson-flow" id="lesson-flow">
    <div class="container">
      <p class="eyebrow">Inside a Lesson</p>
      <h2 class="prog-section__heading" data-animate="reveal-up">What 90 minutes at A-Worthy actually looks like</h2>
      <p class="prog-section__intro" data-animate="reveal-up">Most parents have never seen the inside of a tuition lesson. Here&rsquo;s exactly how a Tuesday-night O-Level English session unfolds &mdash; from the first warm-up question to the homework that gets set before students log off.</p>

      <ol class="lesson-timeline" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="1">
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">0 &ndash; 5 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Retrieval warm-up</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">Five questions on last week&rsquo;s techniques &mdash; vocabulary, grammar, or a quick inference. Students answer in the chat. Anyone who fumbles gets a one-line reminder before we move on. Retrieval is the most underrated study habit, so we build it into every session.</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">5 &ndash; 15 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Question of the week</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">We project a real past-paper question on screen and walk through the <em>See</em> step together. What command word is being used? What text type does the question expect? Which framework will we reach for? By minute fifteen, every student knows what success looks like before they write a single word.</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">15 &ndash; 30 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Framework walkthrough</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">Core Move, ACED, CAPS, STAMP CARD &mdash; whichever framework matches the day&rsquo;s focus. Jeremy demonstrates with a model answer, then deliberately writes a weak version so students can spot the gap. Naming the tool means students can reach for it again on exam day.</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">30 &ndash; 60 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Live writing &amp; in-session feedback</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">Students attempt the question on screen-shared documents. Jeremy moves between answers in real time, flagging issues as they happen &mdash; before bad habits are reinforced. This is where the small class size matters: every student gets at least three feedback touches in thirty minutes.</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">60 &ndash; 80 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Peer marking against the rubric</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">Students swap answers and mark each other&rsquo;s work against the official Cambridge band descriptors. Marking trains the examiner&rsquo;s eye &mdash; the moment a student sees what loses marks in someone else&rsquo;s essay, they stop making the same mistake in their own.</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">80 &ndash; 90 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Exit ticket &amp; week ahead</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">A two-question exit ticket confirms what stuck. Jeremy sets one focused practice piece &mdash; usually fifteen minutes of work &mdash; with a model answer dropped on WhatsApp the next morning. No busywork. Every assignment maps to a specific weakness.</p>
        </li>
      </ol>

      <p class="lesson-flow__note" data-animate="reveal-up">Sessions run weekly via Zoom Pro with cloud recording, so any student who misses a week can catch up before the next one.</p>
    </div>
  </section>

          <div class="faq-answer"><p>Master all four components &mdash; editing, situational writing, continuous writing, and comprehension. Focus on grammar accuracy, vocabulary range, and structured argumentation. The SHARP Method (See the question type, Hit the right framework, Apply it correctly, Refine through feedback, Practise via retrieval) deploys paper-matched frameworks (Core Move, CAPS, P-E-E-L, RAWCP, STAMP CARD) at step H so your child has the right precision tool for every paper section.</p></div>

        </details>
        <details class="faq-item" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="3">
          <summary class="faq-question">What is tested in O-Level English Paper 1?</summary>

        </details>

          <summary class="faq-question">When should I start O-Level English tuition?</summary>

<script is:inline>
(function(){
  var toc = document.getElementById('sticky-toc-list');
  if (!toc) return;
  var sections = document.querySelectorAll('section[id]');
  sections.forEach(function(s) {
    var heading = s.querySelector('h2, h1');
    if (!heading) return;
    var li = document.createElement('li');
    li.className = 'sticky-toc-item';
    var a = document.createElement('a');
    a.className = 'sticky-toc-link';
    a.href = '#' + s.id;
    a.textContent = heading.textContent.substring(0, 30) + (heading.textContent.length > 30 ? '…' : '');
    li.appendChild(a);
    toc.appendChild(li);
  });

  if (!toc.children.length) { document.getElementById('sticky-toc').style.display = 'none'; return; }

  var observer = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
    entries.forEach(function(entry) {
      if (entry.isIntersecting) {
        toc.querySelectorAll('.sticky-toc-item').forEach(function(li) { li.classList.remove('is-active'); });
        toc.querySelectorAll('.sticky-toc-link').forEach(function(a) { a.classList.remove('is-active'); });
        var link = toc.querySelector('a[href="#' + entry.target.id + '"]');
        if (link) { link.classList.add('is-active'); link.parentElement.classList.add('is-active'); }
      }
    });
  }, { threshold: 0.2, rootMargin: '-20% 0px -60% 0px' });
  sections.forEach(function(s) { observer.observe(s); });
})();
</script>

      <h2 class="prog-section__heading" data-animate="reveal-up">Why the SHARP Method is built for General Paper</h2>

      <div class="card-grid card-grid--2">
        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="1">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">See (5 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Your child learns to read every GP question like a lawyer reads a brief &mdash; identifying the command word (discuss, evaluate, assess), the scope of the claim, and the precise angle the examiner is testing. Most students waste time writing about the wrong aspect of the question. This step eliminates that.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="2">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">Hit (10 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Once the question type is clear, your child selects the right framework: P-E-E-L for essay paragraphs, the Evaluation Matrix for balanced arguments, and the AQ Response Template for application questions. Each framework maps directly to what Cambridge examiners check in the mark scheme.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="3">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">Apply (20 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Your child builds a thesis-driven essay or constructs an AQ response using the chosen framework &mdash; with live tutor feedback on argument structure, evidence selection, and evaluative depth. No more wandering paragraphs that start strong and trail off.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="4">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">Refine &amp; Practise (15 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">The steps that separate a C from a B and a B from an A. Your child self-checks against the GP evaluation checklist &mdash; are counter-arguments addressed? Is every example precisely applied, not just name-dropped? Then timed retrieval practice locks the process in under exam conditions.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- ===== INSIDE A LESSON ===== -->
  <section class="prog-section lesson-flow" id="lesson-flow">
    <div class="container">
      <p class="eyebrow">Inside a Lesson</p>
      <h2 class="prog-section__heading" data-animate="reveal-up">What 90 minutes at A-Worthy actually looks like</h2>
      <p class="prog-section__intro" data-animate="reveal-up">Most JC students arrive at GP unsure of what it is they&rsquo;re supposed to <em>do</em>. Here&rsquo;s exactly how a typical A-Worthy GP lesson runs &mdash; from the news brief at the start to the argument bank we set before students log off.</p>

      <ol class="lesson-timeline" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="1">
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">0 &ndash; 5 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">This week in the news</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">We open with three news stories from the past seven days &mdash; one Science &amp; Tech, one Society, one Geopolitics. Students name the GP theme each story maps to. By minute five, every student has three fresh examples they can deploy in this week&rsquo;s essay.</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">5 &ndash; 20 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Question deconstruction</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">A real Cambridge past-paper question goes on screen. We walk through the <em>See</em> step: what&rsquo;s the command word, what&rsquo;s the scope, what counter-claim is the examiner secretly hoping you address? Then the <em>Hit</em> step: which framework wins for this prompt &mdash; P-E-E-L, Evaluation Matrix, or AQ Response Template?</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">20 &ndash; 50 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Live PEEL paragraph drill</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">Students write one full PEEL paragraph in real time. Jeremy moves between answers in the shared document, flagging weak topic sentences, missing evidence and lazy linking phrases as they happen. The point isn&rsquo;t to finish the essay &mdash; it&rsquo;s to get one perfect paragraph that the student can replicate under exam pressure.</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">50 &ndash; 70 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Counter-argument workshop</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">Students pair up and attack each other&rsquo;s argumentation. This is where Band 3 essays become Band 4 &mdash; learning to anticipate and rebut counter-claims is the single biggest mark differentiator in GP. By the end, every student has a stronger argument than the one they started with.</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">70 &ndash; 85 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Examiner&rsquo;s eye</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">We project two unseen sample essays &mdash; one Band 2, one Band 4 &mdash; and students identify what separates them. Learning to mark like an examiner is the fastest way to write like one.</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">85 &ndash; 90 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Argument bank for the week</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">We close by setting one essay plan and one AQ &mdash; both timed, both submitted by Friday for feedback before next session. The week&rsquo;s news examples get added to a running argument bank every student keeps for the year.</p>
        </li>
      </ol>

      <p class="lesson-flow__note" data-animate="reveal-up">Sessions run weekly via Zoom Pro with cloud recording, so any student who misses a week can catch up before the next one.</p>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- ===== SUBJECT TESTIMONIALS ===== -->

  <!-- ===== FAQ ===== -->
  <section class="faq-section" id="faq">
    <div class="container">
      <span class="eyebrow">FAQ</span>
      <h2 class="section-title">Frequently asked questions</h2>
      <div class="faq-list">
        <details class="faq-item" data-animate="reveal-up">
          <summary class="faq-question">How much does GP tuition cost in Singapore?</summary>
          <div class="faq-answer"><p>From SGD 360/month for small group classes of up to 6 students. All essay outlines, comprehension practice sets, and model answers included.</p></div>
        </details>
        <details class="faq-item" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="1">
          <summary class="faq-question">How to score A for General Paper?</summary>
          <div class="faq-answer"><p>Consistent practice across both Paper 1 (essay) and Paper 2 (comprehension). Build a bank of real-world examples, practise writing under timed conditions, and develop a structured approach to AQ answers. The SHARP Method (See, Hit, Apply, Refine, Practise) gives your child a repeatable five-step process for every essay and AQ question, with paper-matched GP frameworks deployed at step H.</p></div>
        </details>
        <details class="faq-item" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="2">
          <summary class="faq-question">Is GP tuition necessary for JC students?</summary>
          <div class="faq-answer"><p>GP is compulsory for the A-Levels and carries significant weight. Many students underestimate it because there is no fixed syllabus. Structured tuition provides the frameworks and content knowledge that self-study often lacks.</p></div>
        </details>
        <details class="faq-item" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="3">
          <summary class="faq-question">What topics come out for GP 2026?</summary>
          <div class="faq-answer"><p>While we cannot predict exact questions, trending themes include AI and technology ethics, climate policy, social media regulation, and inequality. Our programme covers 12 core themes with current affairs updates.</p></div>
        </details>
        <details class="faq-item" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="4">
          <summary class="faq-question">How can I improve my GP comprehension score?</summary>
          <div class="faq-answer"><p>Practise identifying question types (literal, inferential, evaluative), learn paraphrasing techniques, and time yourself strictly. The SHARP Method starts with <em>See</em> &mdash; identifying the question type &mdash; then deploys paper-matched GP frameworks at step <em>Hit</em> to give a systematic approach to each question type.</p></div>
        </details>
      </div>
    </div>
  </section>

<script is:inline>
(function(){
  var toc = document.getElementById('sticky-toc-list');
  if (!toc) return;
  var sections = document.querySelectorAll('section[id]');
  sections.forEach(function(s) {
    var heading = s.querySelector('h2, h1');
    if (!heading) return;
    var li = document.createElement('li');
    li.className = 'sticky-toc-item';
    var a = document.createElement('a');
    a.className = 'sticky-toc-link';
    a.href = '#' + s.id;
    a.textContent = heading.textContent.substring(0, 30) + (heading.textContent.length > 30 ? '…' : '');
    li.appendChild(a);
    toc.appendChild(li);
  });

  if (!toc.children.length) { document.getElementById('sticky-toc').style.display = 'none'; return; }

  var observer = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
    entries.forEach(function(entry) {
      if (entry.isIntersecting) {
        toc.querySelectorAll('.sticky-toc-item').forEach(function(li) { li.classList.remove('is-active'); });
        toc.querySelectorAll('.sticky-toc-link').forEach(function(a) { a.classList.remove('is-active'); });
        var link = toc.querySelector('a[href="#' + entry.target.id + '"]');
        if (link) { link.classList.add('is-active'); link.parentElement.classList.add('is-active'); }
      }
    });
  }, { threshold: 0.2, rootMargin: '-20% 0px -60% 0px' });
  sections.forEach(function(s) { observer.observe(s); });
})();
</script>

  <section class="prog-section" id="approach">
    <div class="container">
      <p class="eyebrow">The SHARP Method</p>
      <h2 class="prog-section__heading" data-animate="reveal-up">Why the SHARP Method produces stronger H2 Economics results</h2>

      <div class="card-grid card-grid--2">
        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="1">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">See (5 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Before writing a single line, your child decodes the question &mdash; is it asking to &ldquo;explain&rdquo; (describe the mechanism), &ldquo;discuss&rdquo; (weigh trade-offs), or &ldquo;evaluate&rdquo; (judge effectiveness with criteria)? They identify the specific economic concepts required, the diagram needed, and the mark allocation. Most students lose marks by answering a &ldquo;discuss&rdquo; question as if it were an &ldquo;explain&rdquo;. This step stops that.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="2">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">Hit (10 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Once the question type is clear, your child selects the right framework: the Diagram-First Approach for theory questions, the DEED structure (Define, Explain, Evaluate, Diagram) for essays, and the Extract-Link-Apply method for case study questions. Each framework is aligned to what Cambridge examiners reward in the 9570 mark scheme.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="3">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">Apply (20 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">Your child constructs a full response &mdash; precise diagrams with correct labelling and shifts, theory explained through cause-and-effect chains, and evaluation that goes beyond &ldquo;it depends on elasticity&rdquo;. Live tutor feedback catches weak economic reasoning before it becomes a habit.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="prog-card" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="4">
          <h3 class="prog-card__title">Refine &amp; Practise (15 min)</h3>
          <p class="prog-card__desc">The step that separates A from B. Your child self-checks every essay against the Economics evaluation checklist &mdash; is the diagram accurate? Are assumptions stated? Is there genuine synthesis, not just listing? Then timed case study drills build the speed and confidence for Paper 1&rsquo;s demanding format.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </section>

  <!-- ===== INSIDE A LESSON ===== -->
  <section class="prog-section lesson-flow" id="lesson-flow">
    <div class="container">
      <p class="eyebrow">Inside a Lesson</p>
      <h2 class="prog-section__heading" data-animate="reveal-up">What 90 minutes at A-Worthy actually looks like</h2>
      <p class="prog-section__intro" data-animate="reveal-up">H2 Economics is where memorisation goes to die. Here&rsquo;s exactly how a typical A-Worthy Economics lesson runs &mdash; built around the case study and essay technique that actually move marks.</p>

      <ol class="lesson-timeline" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="1">
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">0 &ndash; 5 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Diagram speed-draw</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">Five minutes, one diagram from memory &mdash; AD-AS, demand-supply, market failure, exchange rates, or Phillips curve. Students share their attempts on screen. Examiners pay for precise diagrams; we drill until every label, axis and arrow is automatic.</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">5 &ndash; 20 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Case study extract walkthrough</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">We project a real A-Level case study extract on screen. Students underline data, identify economic concepts and predict the questions before reading them. The <em>Extract-Link-Apply</em> framework turns case studies from data dumps into structured arguments.</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">20 &ndash; 40 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">DEED essay framework</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">Define, Explain, Evaluate, Diagram &mdash; the four moves that separate Level 3 answers from Level 2. Jeremy demonstrates with one paragraph from a recent A-Level question, then deliberately writes a weak version so students learn to spot what&rsquo;s missing.</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">40 &ndash; 65 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Live essay writing</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">Students write one full DEED paragraph in real time on a shared document. Jeremy moves between answers and flags issues as they happen &mdash; vague definitions, missing diagrams, evaluation that doesn&rsquo;t actually evaluate. The corrections happen while the thinking is still warm.</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">65 &ndash; 85 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Mark-scheme breakdown</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">We project the SEAB mark scheme alongside two sample answers &mdash; one L2, one L3 &mdash; and identify the exact phrases that earned the upgrade. Learning to read the mark scheme like an examiner is the single biggest mindset shift in Econs.</p>
        </li>
        <li class="lesson-step">
          <span class="lesson-step__time">85 &ndash; 90 min</span>
          <h3 class="lesson-step__title">Retrieval set for the week</h3>
          <p class="lesson-step__desc">We close by setting two timed paragraphs and one diagram retrieval task, both due before next session. The mark scheme phrases from today get added to a running glossary every student keeps for the year.</p>
        </li>
      </ol>

      <p class="lesson-flow__note" data-animate="reveal-up">Sessions run weekly via Zoom Pro with cloud recording, so any student who misses a week can catch up before the next one.</p>
    </div>
  </section>

    <div class="container">
      <span class="eyebrow">FAQ</span>
      <h2 class="section-title">Frequently asked questions</h2>
      <div class="faq-list">
        <details class="faq-item" data-animate="reveal-up">
          <summary class="faq-question">How much does H2 Economics tuition cost in Singapore?</summary>
          <div class="faq-answer"><p>From SGD 360/month for small group classes of up to 6 students. Includes all materials, worksheets, and exam practice papers. No registration or hidden fees.</p></div>
        </details>
        <details class="faq-item" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="1">
          <summary class="faq-question">Is H2 Economics tuition worth it?</summary>
          <div class="faq-answer"><p>Students who join A-Worthy&rsquo;s programme see an average improvement of 2 grades within one term. The SHARP Method (See, Hit, Apply, Refine, Practise) with paper-matched Economics frameworks ensures consistent, measurable progress rather than ad-hoc revision.</p></div>
        </details>
        <details class="faq-item" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="2">
          <summary class="faq-question">What is the difference between H1 and H2 Economics?</summary>
          <div class="faq-answer"><p>H2 Economics covers microeconomics and macroeconomics in greater depth, with a compulsory case study paper. H1 covers similar topics but at a broader level with no case study component.</p></div>
        </details>
        <details class="faq-item" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="3">
          <summary class="faq-question">How can I improve my H2 Economics essays?</summary>
          <div class="faq-answer"><p>Focus on application over theory. Use real-world examples, draw accurate diagrams, and structure essays with clear thesis statements. The SHARP Method gives your child a five-step process (See the question demand, Hit the right structural approach, Apply with precise diagrams and data, Refine through feedback, Practise via retrieval), with paper-matched Economics frameworks deployed at step H for a repeatable structure for essay excellence.</p></div>
        </details>
        <details class="faq-item" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="4">
          <summary class="faq-question">When should I start H2 Economics tuition?</summary>
          <div class="faq-answer"><p>Ideally at the start of JC1 to build strong foundations. However, students joining in JC2 can still see significant improvement with our intensive programme that targets exam-specific skills.</p></div>
        </details>

<script is:inline>
(function(){
  var toc = document.getElementById('sticky-toc-list');
  if (!toc) return;
  var sections = document.querySelectorAll('section[id]');
  sections.forEach(function(s) {
    var heading = s.querySelector('h2, h1');
    if (!heading) return;
    var li = document.createElement('li');
    li.className = 'sticky-toc-item';
    var a = document.createElement('a');
    a.className = 'sticky-toc-link';
    a.href = '#' + s.id;
    a.textContent = heading.textContent.substring(0, 30) + (heading.textContent.length > 30 ? '…' : '');
    li.appendChild(a);
    toc.appendChild(li);
  });

  if (!toc.children.length) { document.getElementById('sticky-toc').style.display = 'none'; return; }

  var observer = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
    entries.forEach(function(entry) {
      if (entry.isIntersecting) {
        toc.querySelectorAll('.sticky-toc-item').forEach(function(li) { li.classList.remove('is-active'); });
        toc.querySelectorAll('.sticky-toc-link').forEach(function(a) { a.classList.remove('is-active'); });
        var link = toc.querySelector('a[href="#' + entry.target.id + '"]');
        if (link) { link.classList.add('is-active'); link.parentElement.classList.add('is-active'); }
      }
    });
  }, { threshold: 0.2, rootMargin: '-20% 0px -60% 0px' });
  sections.forEach(function(s) { observer.observe(s); });
})();
</script>

<script is:inline>
(function(){
  var cards = document.querySelectorAll('.journey-card');
  if (!cards.length) return;
  var observer = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
    entries.forEach(function(entry) {
      if (entry.isIntersecting) {
        entry.target.classList.add('is-visible');
        observer.unobserve(entry.target);
      }
    });
  }, { threshold: 0.3 });
  cards.forEach(function(c) { observer.observe(c); });
})();
</script>

================================================================================

import BaseLayout from '../layouts/BaseLayout.astro';
import Header from '../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../components/Footer.astro';
import '../styles/global.css';

const stories = [
  {
    name: 'Sarah T.',
    before: 'C5',
    after: 'A2',
    duration: '3 months',
    subject: 'O-Level English',
    quote: '"I used to dread comprehension passages. Now I actually enjoy pulling them apart — it\'s like solving a puzzle."',
    quoteAttr: '— Sarah T., Sec 4',
    paragraphs: [
      'When Sarah first joined A-Worthy, she struggled most with inference questions and summary writing. Her answers were vague and lacked the precision examiners look for. She would often write what she felt the passage meant rather than what the text actually supported.',
      'Through the SHARP Method, Sarah learned to treat every comprehension passage like a legal brief — identifying key claims, tracing the author\'s argument, and backing every answer with direct textual evidence. Her tutor worked with her weekly on structured annotation techniques that made even the trickiest inference questions approachable.',
      'By her third month, the transformation was unmistakable. Sarah\'s summary scores jumped from 4/8 to 7/8 consistently, and her overall English grade moved from C5 to A2. More importantly, she developed a confidence in analytical reading that carried over to her other subjects.'

<script is:inline>
(function(){
  var track = document.getElementById('carousel-track');
  var dots = document.getElementById('carousel-dots');
  if (!track || !dots) return;
  var slides = track.querySelectorAll('.carousel-slide');
  var count = slides.length;
  var current = 0;

  // Create dots
  for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    var dot = document.createElement('button');
    dot.className = 'carousel-dot' + (i === 0 ? ' is-active' : '');
    dot.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Go to testimonial ' + (i + 1));
    dot.setAttribute('data-index', i);
    dots.appendChild(dot);
  }

  function goTo(idx) {
    current = idx;
    track.style.transform = 'translateX(-' + (current * 100) + '%)';
    dots.querySelectorAll('.carousel-dot').forEach(function(d, i) {
      d.classList.toggle('is-active', i === current);
    });
  }

  dots.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    var dot = e.target.closest('.carousel-dot');
    if (dot) goTo(parseInt(dot.getAttribute('data-index')));
  });

  // Auto-rotate every 6 seconds
  var timer = setInterval(function() {
    goTo((current + 1) % count);
  }, 6000);

  // Pause on hover
  track.parentElement.addEventListener('mouseenter', function() { clearInterval(timer); });
  track.parentElement.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
    timer = setInterval(function() { goTo((current + 1) % count); }, 6000);
  });
})();
</script>

      <h2 class="section-title" data-animate="reveal-up">Frequently Asked Questions</h2>
      <div class="faq-list" data-animate="reveal-up" data-animate-delay="1">
        <details class="faq-item">
          <summary class="faq-question">Are there any registration or material fees?</summary>
          <p class="faq-answer">No. The monthly fee covers everything &mdash; lesson materials, practice papers, model answers, and access to the resource vault. There are no hidden fees.</p>
        </details>
        <details class="faq-item">
          <summary class="faq-question">Is there a lock-in contract?</summary>
          <p class="faq-answer">No. All programmes are month-to-month. You can stop at any time with no penalty &mdash; we believe in earning your trust every month.</p>
        </details>
        <details class="faq-item">
          <summary class="faq-question">Why is the fee range (e.g. SGD 280&ndash;320) instead of a fixed price?</summary>
          <p class="faq-answer">The lower end is for Sec 1&ndash;2 or JC 1 foundation programmes, and the higher end is for Sec 3&ndash;4 or JC 2 intensive programmes, which include more exam-focused content and additional practice materials.</p>
        </details>
        <details class="faq-item">
          <summary class="faq-question">How does the money-back guarantee work?</summary>
          <p class="faq-answer">If you&rsquo;re not satisfied after the first month of lessons, contact us within 7 days of the last session and we&rsquo;ll issue a full refund &mdash; no questions asked.</p>
        </details>
        <details class="faq-item">
          <summary class="faq-question">Can I switch between group and 1-to-1 coaching?</summary>
          <p class="faq-answer">Yes. Many students start with group sessions and add occasional 1-to-1 coaching closer to exams. You can mix and match as needed.</p>
        </details>
        <details class="faq-item">
          <summary class="faq-question">Are there sibling or multi-subject discounts?</summary>
          <p class="faq-answer">Yes, we offer a 10% sibling discount and a 5% discount for students enrolled in two or more subjects. Contact us for details.</p>
        </details>
      </div>
    </div>
  </section>

<script>
  const searchInput = document.getElementById('resource-search') as HTMLInputElement;
  const filterButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.r-filter-btn');
  const resourceCards = document.querySelectorAll('.r-card') as NodeListOf<HTMLElement>;
  const noResults = document.getElementById('no-results') as HTMLElement;

  let activeCategory = 'All';

  function filterResources() {
    const searchTerm = searchInput.value.toLowerCase().trim();
    let visibleCount = 0;

    resourceCards.forEach((card) => {
      const title = card.getAttribute('data-title') || '';
      const description = card.getAttribute('data-description') || '';
      const category = card.getAttribute('data-category') || '';

      const matchesCategory = activeCategory === 'All' || category === activeCategory;
      const matchesSearch = !searchTerm || title.includes(searchTerm) || description.includes(searchTerm);

      if (matchesCategory && matchesSearch) {
        card.style.display = '';
        visibleCount++;
      } else {
        card.style.display = 'none';
      }
    });

    noResults.style.display = visibleCount === 0 ? 'flex' : 'none';
  }

  searchInput.addEventListener('input', filterResources);

  filterButtons.forEach((btn) => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      filterButtons.forEach((b) => b.classList.remove('active'));
      btn.classList.add('active');
      activeCategory = btn.getAttribute('data-category') || 'All';
      filterResources();
    });
  });

  const newsletterForm = document.getElementById('newsletter-form') as HTMLFormElement;
  const newsletterSuccess = document.getElementById('newsletter-success') as HTMLElement;
  const newsletterSubmit = document.getElementById('newsletter-submit') as HTMLButtonElement;

  newsletterForm?.addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const emailInput = document.getElementById('newsletter-email') as HTMLInputElement;
    if (!emailInput.value) return;

    newsletterSubmit.disabled = true;
    newsletterSubmit.textContent = 'Subscribing...';

    try {
      const formData = new FormData(newsletterForm);
      const response = await fetch(newsletterForm.action, {
        method: 'POST',
        body: formData,
        headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json' },
      });

      if (response.ok) {
        emailInput.value = '';
        newsletterSuccess.hidden = false;
      } else {
        throw new Error('Failed');
      }
    } catch {
      newsletterSuccess.hidden = false;
      newsletterSuccess.textContent = 'Something went wrong. Please try again.';
    } finally {
      newsletterSubmit.disabled = false;
      newsletterSubmit.textContent = 'Subscribe';
    }
  });
</script>

<script is:inline>
(function(){
  var FORMSPREE_ID = 'xreoozkk';
  var FORMSPREE_URL = 'https://formspree.io/f/' + FORMSPREE_ID;

  function getStoredLead() {
    try {
      var raw = localStorage.getItem('resource-lead');
      return raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : null;
    } catch (e) { return null; }
  }

  function storeLead(email, phone, name) {
    try {
      localStorage.setItem('resource-lead', JSON.stringify({ email: email, phone: phone, name: name || '' }));
    } catch (e) {}
  }

  function submitLead(payload) {
    return fetch(FORMSPREE_URL, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json', 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify(payload)
    });
  }

  function showToast(message) {
    var toast = document.createElement('div');
    toast.className = 'resource-toast';
    toast.textContent = message;
    document.body.appendChild(toast);
    setTimeout(function() { toast.classList.add('resource-toast--show'); }, 10);
    setTimeout(function() {
      toast.classList.remove('resource-toast--show');
      setTimeout(function() { toast.remove(); }, 300);
    }, 4500);
  }

  function deliverResource(mode, url, title) {
    if (mode === 'download' && url) {
      window.open(url, '_blank');
      showToast('Sample opened in a new tab. The full version of "' + title + '" will be emailed shortly.');
    } else {
      showToast('Thanks! We’ll email the full version of "' + title + '" within 24 hours.');
    }
  }

  function openGate(mode, url, title) {
    var overlay = document.createElement('div');
    overlay.className = 'resource-gate-overlay';
    var ctaLabel = mode === 'download' ? 'Send me the resource' : 'Email me the full version';
    var heading = mode === 'download'
      ? 'Get instant access to your A-Worthy resource'
      : 'Request the full version of this resource';
    var subline = mode === 'download'
      ? 'Enter your details to preview the sample now. We’ll also email the full version of "' + title + '" to you.'
      : 'Enter your details and we’ll email "' + title + '" to you within 24 hours.';

    var waMessage = encodeURIComponent('Hi A-Worthy, I would like the full version of "' + title + '". Could you send it to me?');
    var waUrl = 'https://wa.me/6583384033?text=' + waMessage;

    overlay.innerHTML =
      '<div class="resource-gate" role="dialog" aria-modal="true" aria-labelledby="resource-gate-title">' +
        '<button class="resource-gate-close" aria-label="Close">&times;</button>' +
        '<span class="resource-gate-eyebrow">Free Resource</span>' +
        '<h4 id="resource-gate-title">' + heading + '</h4>' +
        '<p>' + subline + '</p>' +
        '<form class="resource-gate-form" novalidate>' +
          '<label class="resource-gate-label">' +
            '<span>Email <em>*</em></span>' +
            '<input type="email" name="email" required autocomplete="email" placeholder="you@email.com" />' +
          '</label>' +
          '<label class="resource-gate-label">' +
            '<span>Phone (Singapore) <em>*</em></span>' +
            '<input type="tel" name="phone" required autocomplete="tel" inputmode="tel" placeholder="+65 9123 4567" />' +
          '</label>' +
          '<label class="resource-gate-label">' +
            '<span>Name <em class="resource-gate-optional">(optional)</em></span>' +
            '<input type="text" name="name" autocomplete="name" placeholder="Parent or student name" />' +
          '</label>' +
          '<button type="submit" class="resource-gate-submit">' + ctaLabel + '</button>' +
          '<p class="resource-gate-error" hidden></p>' +
          '<p class="resource-gate-note">We respect your privacy. No spam &mdash; unsubscribe anytime.</p>' +
        '</form>' +
        '<div class="resource-gate-divider"><span>or</span></div>' +
        '<a class="resource-gate-whatsapp" href="' + waUrl + '" target="_blank" rel="noopener">' +
          '<svg aria-hidden="true" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor"><path d="M.057 24l1.687-6.163c-1.041-1.804-1.588-3.849-1.587-5.946.003-6.556 5.338-11.891 11.893-11.891 3.181.001 6.167 1.24 8.413 3.488 2.245 2.248 3.481 5.236 3.48 8.414-.003 6.557-5.338 11.892-11.893 11.892-1.99-.001-3.951-.5-5.688-1.448l-6.305 1.654zm6.597-3.807c1.676.995 3.276 1.591 5.392 1.592 5.448 0 9.886-4.434 9.889-9.885.002-5.462-4.415-9.89-9.881-9.892-5.452 0-9.887 4.434-9.889 9.884-.001 2.225.651 3.891 1.746 5.634l-.999 3.648 3.742-.981zm11.387-5.464c-.074-.124-.272-.198-.57-.347-.297-.149-1.758-.868-2.031-.967-.272-.099-.47-.149-.669.149-.198.297-.768.967-.941 1.165-.173.198-.347.223-.644.074-.297-.149-1.255-.462-2.39-1.475-.883-.788-1.48-1.761-1.653-2.059-.173-.297-.018-.458.13-.606.134-.133.297-.347.446-.521.151-.172.2-.296.3-.495.099-.198.05-.371-.025-.52-.075-.149-.669-1.612-.916-2.207-.242-.579-.487-.5-.669-.51l-.57-.01c-.198 0-.52.074-.792.372s-1.04 1.016-1.04 2.479 1.065 2.876 1.213 3.074c.149.198 2.095 3.2 5.076 4.487.711.307 1.265.489 1.697.626.713.226 1.362.194 1.875.118.572-.085 1.758-.719 2.006-1.413.248-.694.248-1.289.173-1.413z"/></svg>' +
          'Get it instantly on WhatsApp' +
        '</a>' +
      '</div>';

    document.body.appendChild(overlay);
    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';

    function close() {
      overlay.remove();
      document.body.style.overflow = '';
    }

    overlay.querySelector('.resource-gate-close').addEventListener('click', close);
    overlay.addEventListener('click', function(ev) {
      if (ev.target === overlay) close();
    });
    document.addEventListener('keydown', function escHandler(ev) {
      if (ev.key === 'Escape') { close(); document.removeEventListener('keydown', escHandler); }
    });

    setTimeout(function() {
      var firstInput = overlay.querySelector('input[name="email"]');
      if (firstInput) firstInput.focus();
    }, 50);

    var form = overlay.querySelector('form');
    var submitBtn = overlay.querySelector('.resource-gate-submit');
    var errorEl = overlay.querySelector('.resource-gate-error');

    form.addEventListener('submit', function(ev) {
      ev.preventDefault();
      var email = form.email.value.trim();
      var phone = form.phone.value.trim();
      var name = form.name.value.trim();

      var phoneDigits = phone.replace(/\D/g, '');
      if (!email || !/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email)) {
        errorEl.textContent = 'Please enter a valid email address.';
        errorEl.hidden = false;
        return;
      }
      if (phoneDigits.length < 8) {
        errorEl.textContent = 'Please enter a valid phone number.';
        errorEl.hidden = false;
        return;
      }
      errorEl.hidden = true;

      submitBtn.disabled = true;
      submitBtn.textContent = 'Sending...';

      var payload = {
        email: email,
        phone: phone,
        name: name,
        resource: title,
        mode: mode,
        _subject: 'Resource Download Request: ' + title
      };

      submitLead(payload).then(function(res) {
        if (!res.ok) throw new Error('submit-failed');
        storeLead(email, phone, name);
        close();
        deliverResource(mode, url, title);
      }).catch(function() {
        // Still store locally and deliver so the user isn't blocked by a Formspree outage.
        storeLead(email, phone, name);
        close();
        deliverResource(mode, url, title);
      });
    });
  }

  function handleClick(e) {
    var el = e.currentTarget;
    var mode = el.getAttribute('data-resource-mode');
    var title = el.getAttribute('data-resource-title') || 'A-Worthy resource';
    var url = el.getAttribute('href');
    var stored = getStoredLead();

    if (stored && stored.email && stored.phone) {
      // Returning visitor: silently log the request and deliver.
      submitLead({
        email: stored.email,
        phone: stored.phone,
        name: stored.name || '',
        resource: title,
        mode: mode,
        repeat: true,
        _subject: 'Resource Re-download: ' + title
      }).catch(function() {});

      if (mode === 'request') {
        e.preventDefault();
        deliverResource(mode, url, title);
      }
      // For mode === 'download', let the native <a download> open the file.
      return;
    }

    e.preventDefault();
    openGate(mode, url, title);
  }

  document.querySelectorAll('[data-resource-mode]').forEach(function(el) {
    el.addEventListener('click', handleClick);
  });
})();
</script>

<style>
  .resource-gate-overlay {
    position: fixed;
    inset: 0;
    background: rgba(0,0,0,0.55);
    z-index: 2000;
    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    padding: 1rem;
    -webkit-backdrop-filter: blur(6px);
    backdrop-filter: blur(6px);
  }
  .resource-gate {
    background: var(--bg-primary);
    border: 1px solid var(--border-color);
    border-radius: 12px;
    padding: 2rem 1.75rem 1.5rem;
    max-width: 420px;
    width: 100%;
    position: relative;
    box-shadow: 0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.25);
  }
  .resource-gate-close {
    position: absolute;
    top: 0.5rem;
    right: 0.75rem;
    background: none;
    border: none;
    font-size: 1.5rem;
    line-height: 1;

<!-- ===== CLIENT-SIDE SCRIPTS ===== -->
<script>
  // --- Form Validation & Submission ---
  const form = document.getElementById('contact-form') as HTMLFormElement;
  const successMsg = document.getElementById('form-success') as HTMLDivElement;
  const errorsMsg = document.getElementById('form-errors') as HTMLDivElement;

  form.addEventListener('submit', async (e: Event) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const errors: string[] = [];

    const parentName = (form.querySelector('#parent-name') as HTMLInputElement).value.trim();
    const studentName = (form.querySelector('#student-name') as HTMLInputElement).value.trim();
    const email = (form.querySelector('#email') as HTMLInputElement).value.trim();
    const phone = (form.querySelector('#phone') as HTMLInputElement).value.trim();
    const studentLevel = (form.querySelector('#student-level') as HTMLSelectElement).value;
    if (!parentName) errors.push('Parent/Guardian Name is required.');
    if (!studentName) errors.push('Student Name is required.');
    if (!email) {
      errors.push('Email is required.');
    } else if (!/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]{2,}$/.test(email)) {
      errors.push('Please enter a valid email address.');
    }
    if (!phone) {
      errors.push('Phone Number is required.');
    } else if (!/^\+?[\d][\d\s\-()]{6,14}$/.test(phone)) {
      errors.push('Please enter a valid phone number.');
    }
    if (!studentLevel) errors.push('Please select a Student Level.');

    if (errors.length > 0) {
      errorsMsg.hidden = false;
      errorsMsg.textContent = '';
      errors.forEach(err => {
        const p = document.createElement('p');
        p.textContent = err;
        errorsMsg.appendChild(p);
      });
      successMsg.hidden = true;
      errorsMsg.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
      return;
    }

    // Submit form data
    var submitBtn = document.getElementById('form-submit-btn') as HTMLButtonElement;
    submitBtn.disabled = true;
    submitBtn.innerHTML = '<span class="spinner"></span> Sending...';

    try {
      const formData = new FormData(form);
      const response = await fetch(form.action, {
        method: 'POST',
        body: formData,
        headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json' },
      });

      if (response.ok) {
        errorsMsg.hidden = true;
        successMsg.hidden = false;
        form.reset();
        successMsg.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
      } else {
        throw new Error('Submission failed');
      }
    } catch {
      errorsMsg.hidden = false;
      errorsMsg.textContent = '';
      const p = document.createElement('p');
      p.textContent = 'Something went wrong. Please try again or contact us via WhatsApp.';
      errorsMsg.appendChild(p);
      successMsg.hidden = true;
      errorsMsg.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
    } finally {
      submitBtn.disabled = false;
      submitBtn.innerHTML = '<span>Find Out How We Can Help</span>';
    }
  });

  // --- FAQ Accordion (single-open) ---
  document.querySelectorAll('.faq-question').forEach((btn) => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      const item = btn.parentElement as HTMLDivElement;
      const answer = item.querySelector('.faq-answer') as HTMLDivElement;
      const isOpen = btn.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true';

      // Close all others
      document.querySelectorAll('.faq-item').forEach((otherItem) => {
        if (otherItem !== item) {
          const otherBtn = otherItem.querySelector('.faq-question') as HTMLButtonElement;
          const otherAnswer = otherItem.querySelector('.faq-answer') as HTMLDivElement;
          otherBtn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
          otherAnswer.hidden = true;
          otherItem.classList.remove('is-open');
        }
      });

      // Toggle current
      btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', String(!isOpen));
      answer.hidden = isOpen;
      item.classList.toggle('is-open', !isOpen);
    });
  });
</script>

FILE: src/pages/accessibility.astro

---
import BaseLayout from '../layouts/BaseLayout.astro';
import Header from '../components/Header.astro';
import Footer from '../components/Footer.astro';
import '../styles/global.css';
---

<BaseLayout title="Accessibility | A-Worthy" description="A-Worthy's commitment to web accessibility. Learn about our efforts to make our website usable for everyone.">
  <Header slot="header" />

  <section class="section">
    <div class="container a11y-content">
      <span class="eyebrow">Accessibility</span>
      <h1 class="a11y-title">Accessibility Statement</h1>

      <p>A-Worthy is committed to ensuring our website is accessible to all users, including those with disabilities. We strive to meet <strong>WCAG 2.2 Level AA</strong> standards.</p>

      <h2>What we do</h2>
      <ul>
        <li>Semantic HTML with proper heading hierarchy</li>
        <li>ARIA labels on all interactive elements</li>
        <li>Keyboard navigation support throughout the site</li>
        <li>Sufficient colour contrast ratios in both light and dark modes</li>
        <li>Reduced motion support for users who prefer less animation</li>
        <li>High contrast mode compatibility</li>
        <li>Screen reader compatible content structure</li>
        <li>Skip-to-content link for keyboard users</li>
      </ul>

      <h2>Known limitations</h2>
      <p>Some PDF resources may not be fully screen-reader compatible. We are working to improve this. Our video content (when available) will include captions.</p>

      <h2>Feedback</h2>
      <p>If you encounter any accessibility barriers on our website, please <a href="/contact/">contact us</a>. We take all feedback seriously and will work to address any issues promptly.</p>

      <p class="a11y-updated">This statement was last updated in April 2026.</p>
    </div>
  </section>

  <Footer slot="footer" />
</BaseLayout>
